7         point. I would need to go away and look at the numbers                    7                      (The hearing adjourned until 10 am
8         and look at the availability of tests to see whether                      8                            on Thursday, 14 March 2024)
9         that was a practical proposition, but as a basic                          9
10        proposition: you haven't got many tests but you don't                    10
11        need many of them for this group, you know, it's                         11
12        a reasonable point to make.                                              12
13   LADY HALLETT: And we know how vulnerable people in                            13
14        care homes are.                                                          14
15   A.   We do.                                                                   15
16   MR STRAW: Thank you.                                                          16
17   LADY HALLETT: Thank you, Mr Straw.                                            17
18            Does that complete the questioning?                                  18
19   MR POOLE: It does, my Lady, yes.                                              19
20   LADY HALLETT: Mr Drakeford, thank you very much indeed for                    20
21        your help, both in this module and the previous module.                  21
22        I don't know what life has in store for you when you                     22
23        step down as First Minister, but obviously we wish you                   23
24        well. Thank you.                                                         24
25   THE WITNESS: Thank you.                                                       25
